    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; For the purposes of this test program, the machine state consists of:"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":";\ta 2 byte memory operand, followed by"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":";\tthe registers iy,ix,hl,de,bc,af,sp"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; for a total of 16 bytes."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; The program tests instructions (or groups of similar instructions)"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; by cycling through a sequence of machine states, executing the test"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; instruction for each one and running a 32-bit crc over the resulting"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; machine states.  At the end of the sequence the crc is compared to"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; an expected value that was found empirically on a real Z80."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; A test case is defined by a descriptor which consists of:"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":";\ta flag mask byte,"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":";\tthe base case,"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":";\tthe incement vector,"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":";\tthe shift vector,"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":";\tthe expected crc,"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":";\ta short descriptive message."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":";"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; The flag mask byte is used to prevent undefined flag bits from"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; influencing the results.  Documented flags are as per Mostek Z80"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; Technical Manual."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":";"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; The next three parts of the descriptor are 20 byte vectors"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; corresponding to a 4 byte instruction and a 16 byte machine state."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; The first part is the base case, which is the first test case of"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; the sequence.  This base is then modified according to the next 2"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; vectors.  Each 1 bit in the increment vector specifies a bit to be"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; cycled in the form of a binary counter.  For instance, if the byte"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; corresponding to the accumulator is set to 0ffh in the increment"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; vector, the test will be repeated for all 256 values of the"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; accumulator.  Note that 1 bits don't have to be contiguous.  The"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; number of test cases 'caused' by the increment vector is equal to"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; 2^(number of 1 bits).  The shift vector is similar, but specifies a"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; set of bits in the test case that are to be successively inverted."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; Thus the shift vector 'causes' a number of test cases equal to the"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; number of 1 bits in it."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; The total number of test cases is the product of those caused by the"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; counter and shift vectors and can easily become unweildy.  Each"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; individual test case can take a few milliseconds to execute, due to"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; the overhead of test setup and crc calculation, so test design is a"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; compromise between coverage and execution time."
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; This program is designed to detect differences between"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; implementations and is not ideal for diagnosing the causes of any"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; discrepancies.  However, provided a reference implementation (or"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; real system) is available, a failing test case can be isolated by"
    },
    {
        "type":"newline",
        "value":"\r\n"
    },
    {
        "type":"comment",
        "value":"; hand using a binary search of the test space."
    },

        "value":"\r\n"
